--++ (0,2) node [above right] {$C_1$} coordinate (C1)
--++ (-2,0) node [above left] {$D_1$} coordinate (D1) --++ (225:{2/2}) node [left] {$A_1$} coordinate (A1) -- cycle;

\end{tikzpicture}
